Reporting and enforcement
=========================

Learn about reporting content on YouTube, the actions our teams take when reviewing content, and what this means for you.

Reporting
---------

*   [Report inappropriate videos, channels, and other content on YouTube](/youtube/answer/2802027?hl=en&ref_topic=9387085)
*   [Report a YouTube search prediction](/youtube/answer/7626105?hl=en&ref_topic=9387085)
*   [Other reporting options](/youtube/answer/2802057?hl=en&ref_topic=9387085)
*   [About the YouTube Trusted Flagger program](/youtube/answer/7554338?hl=en&ref_topic=9387085)
*   [Report policy-violative ads](/youtube/answer/10684207?hl=en&ref_topic=9387085)
